JAKHARIA FABRIC LIMITED    JAKHARIA : Related Party Transactions Non applicability of Disclosure on Related Party Transactions for Half Year Ended 30th September, 2020

Dear Sir / Madam, 

This is to inform you that Disclosure on Related Party Transactions for Half Year Ended 30th September, 2020 under Regulation 23(9) of SEBI (Listing Obligations and Disclosure Requirements) (Amendment) Regulation, 2018 is not applicable to our company.
Further, We would like to clarify that our company is claiming exemption under Regulation 15 (2) of SEBI (Listing Obligations and Disclosure Requirements) Regulations, 2015 as corporate Governance provision shall not apply to listed entity which has listed its specified securities on the SME Exchange.
Since, our company is exempted under Regulation 15(2) of SEBI (Listing Obligations and Disclosure Requirements) Regulations, 2015; we are not submitting Disclosure on Related Party Transactions for Half Year Ended 30th September, 2020.

Kindly update the above in your records.
